msg:The Hyatt Hotel Global Harbor is located in the city center, on the bank of Suzhou River, with convenient transportation. It can be directly transferred to Metro Line 4 and Line 13. It is just across the road from Tuotie Exit 2. If it rains, you can go to Global Harbor Mall through Exit 1 indoors.
The hotel has complete facilities, dry and wet separation, a large bathtub, and a shower room, where two people can take a bath at the same time without interfering with each other.
The hotel service responds quickly and efficiently. I called for water at 10:30 in the evening, and it was delivered as soon as I put down the phone.
Our family has stayed in this hotel for many years. In addition to the hotel... advanced facilities, clean and sanitary, first-class service, Global Harbor Mall has many shopping malls and European-style environment from the second underground floor to the upper floors, and there is also the Sega Amusement Park that children and adults are thinking about.

msg:This is the third time I stayed at the Hyatt Regency Global Center. I checked in late, so the front desk upgraded me to a suite. The space doubled directly, with a double basin smart toilet and a comfortable living room surround. I have to give this praise.
I stayed in the city view king room last time. It was well lit and large, which was completely sufficient for use.
Hotel advantages:
Geographic location: Located in the Global Center, the subway station is right at the door. Whether it is Huaihai Middle Road or Xintiandi, it is relatively close to take a taxi to the subway. There is a shopping mall downstairs of the hotel. There are basically all normal brands, and it is also very convenient to eat, drink and have fun. There are no luxury brands or very popular restaurants in the mall. If you like, you can go out and find them, and it won‚Äôt be far.
Hotel environment: clean and comfortable, the items are well maintained, and the texture is not old. It has been opened for some years and the occupancy rate should not be low, so the items have traces of use, but relatively speaking, they are well maintained, so the texture is not bad.
Room facilities: The facilities of the basic room are obviously older than other room types. The first time I checked in, I entered a twin bed room with a strong smell of smoke. It was much better after the replacement. The second time, the city view bed was more comfortable. This time the suite was cleaner and tidier. Not only the area and facilities were upgraded with different levels, but there was also a more obvious difference between the old and the new.
Service attitude: It's quite standard, everything is there, the welcome service and farewell are all in place.
Thanks to all the staff for their concerted efforts, the three stays are better than the last, thank you for the upgrade~

The hotel check-in procedure is on the 7th floor. You can take the elevator directly to the 7th floor, which is very convenient.

Room service and catering services are very good and the service attitude is very good. This is a warm hotel.

msg:I booked a room one day in advance for Valentine's Day and chose the basic room type - Hyatt King Room. I chose this hotel because I thought the price was okay, just over 1k including breakfast for two, and because I thought the hotel was connected to a shopping mall, where there were places to play and the kids wouldn't be bored.

The check-in time is after 15:00, but I actually got a room at 14:00. The kid was given a little tiger doll in Shanghai cheongsam when he checked in. The 3*** room has a reasonable structure, and the places to put luggage and boil water are very convenient, nothing fancy.

It's basically necessary to let the kid swim when taking him out. The hotel swimming pool is not big, but it is 25 meters long and the water temperature is 28 degrees, which is not bad.

It's worth praising their breakfast, which costs more than 100 yuan per adult, with rich varieties, bread, juice, and hot dishes. One of them is a black truffle egg fried rice, which is very fragrant and can definitely be used as brunch when getting up late. And the kids were very happy after drinking a few Yakults...

The only drawback of the hotel is that the parking fee is self-paid, 120 yuan for more than 8 hours and within 24 hours.
